href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/how-to-make-dukkah/\">How to Make Authentic Dukkah in Four Easy Steps</a></h2><p class=\"post-meta\"> <span class=\"tie-date\"><i class=\"fa fa-clock-o\"></i>6 days ago</span> <span class=\"post-comments\"><i class=\"fa fa-comments\"></i><a href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/how-to-make-dukkah/#respond\">0</a></span></p><div class=\"post-thumbnail\"> <a href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/how-to-make-dukkah/\"> <img width=\"250\" height=\"250\" src=\"https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Dukkah-thumb-2-250x250.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail wp-post-image pib-hover-img\" alt=\"How to Make Authentic Dukkah in Four Easy Steps - take your spices to the next level | hurrythefoodup.com\" srcset=\"https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Dukkah-thumb-2-250x250.jpg 250w, https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Dukkah-thumb-2-300x300.jpg 300w, https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Dukkah-thumb-2.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 250px) 100vw, 250px\" data-pin-url=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/how-to-make-dukkah/\"> <span class=\"fa overlay-icon\"></span> </a></div><div class=\"entry\"><p>Before we get into to the hows of Dukkah, let’s take a look at the whats. Every now and then a complete game-changer comes along, and Dukkah is one of them. An incredible fusion of nuts, herbs, seeds and spices, it’s an easy to make mix that can completely revitalise …</p> <a class=\"more-link\" href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/how-to-make-dukkah/\">Read More »</a></div><div class=\"clear\"></div> </article><article class=\"item-list\"><h2 class=\"post-box-title\"> <a href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/roasted-cauliflower-curry/\">Roasted Cauliflower Curry | Sweet, Spicy and Vegan – Pakistani Style</a></h2><p class=\"post-meta\"> <span class=\"tie-date\"><i class=\"fa fa-clock-o\"></i>2 weeks ago</span> <span class=\"post-comments\"><i class=\"fa fa-comments\"></i><a href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/roasted-cauliflower-curry/#comments\">3</a></span></p><div class=\"post-thumbnail\"> <a href=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/roasted-cauliflower-curry/\"> <img width=\"250\" height=\"250\" src=\"https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/roasted-cauliflower-curry-thumb-1-250x250.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail wp-post-image pib-hover-img\" alt=\"Roasted Cauliflower Curry | Sweet, Spicy and Vegan - Pakistani Style. A delicious fusion of Pakistani spices | hurrythefoodup.com\" srcset=\"https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/roasted-cauliflower-curry-thumb-1-250x250.jpg 250w, https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/roasted-cauliflower-curry-thumb-1-300x300.jpg 300w, https://cdn.hurrythefoodup.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/roasted-cauliflower-curry-thumb-1.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 250px) 100vw, 250px\" data-pin-url=\"https://hurrythefoodup.com/roasted-cauliflower-curry/\"> <span class=\"fa overlay-icon\"></span> </a></div><div class=\"entry\"><p>It must be that time of year.
